NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING

WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
MOTONIC INDIA AUTOMOTIVE PRIVATE LIMITED
Survey No. 200/5A, 5B, 10 & 11, Vayalur Village, Thiruvallur Taluk and District.
Thiruvallur-602 105, Tamil Nadu
CIN No. U29220TN2008PTC066007
Phone No. +91 72999 87003

NOTICE OF MEETINGS OF SHAREHOLDERS AND CREDITORS
Notice is hereby given that,
(1.) A meeting of the Shareholders of the Company will be held at 200/5A, 5B, 10 & 11, Vayalur Village,
Thiruvallur Taluk and District, Thiruvallur-602 105 Tamil Nadu on Monday, the 17th day of August 2015 at 11 a.m.
to consider the Annual Accounts, Voluntary Winding up subject to approval by the Creditors and appointment of
Mr. Saji P John, Advocate to be the Liquidator of the Company.
(2.)A meeting of the creditors of the Company will be held at 200/5A, 5B, 10 & 11, Vayalur Village, Thiruvallur
Taluk and District, Thiruvallur-602 105 Tamil Nadu on Monday, the 17th day of August 2015 at 12 p.m. to consider
Creditor’s Voluntarily Winding up under Section 499 and 500 of the Companies Act and to approve appointment
of Mr. Saji P John, Advocate to be the Liquidator of the Company.
Note: The Statement of Affairs of the Company and the list of creditors of the Company are available for
inspection at the venue of the meeting subject to proving the identity of the Creditor.

Motonic India Automotive Private Limited,
Thiruvallur,
27th July 2015.

HYEONGDEOK KIM,
Managing Director.
